**Architect — Insight-205 captured: Battle-Ready Project Onboarding (2026-04-25, architect checkpoint #3):** User steer mid-Brief-212-session: "when we connect to a new project repo, we should run an in-depth analysis on the project and retro-fit or augment a harness and skill and tool system into the project to make sure the project is battle ready." Captured as `docs/insights/205-battle-ready-project-onboarding.md`. **The insight:** the harness does NOT stop at Ditto's boundary — it extends into every repo Ditto manages. Connecting a project is a multi-step PROCESS (Research → Design → Build → Review applied to a *project*, not a Ditto feature), not a metadata operation. Existing Ditto roles map cleanly: `/dev-researcher` runs the in-depth analysis (build system, test framework, CI status, existing harness/skills/tools, persona-fit), `/dev-architect` produces the retrofit plan, `/dev-builder` executes via Brief 212's bridge (local-mac-mini) or `claude-code-routine` (cloud) or `github-action`, `/dev-reviewer` audits, `/dev-documenter` records project memories. **Durable artefacts:** retrofitter writes a `.ditto/` directory IN the target repo (role contracts, skill index, tool allowlist, project-specific guidance) — honours Insight-201 (user-facing legibility — grep-able where the work happens) AND Insight-202 (Ditto-as-X before external-X — Ditto provides the in-repo substrate without requiring the project to install Ditto code). **Trust-tier-bound retrofit depth:** supervised approves every file, autonomous retrofits silently and user audits the diff after, critical rejected. **Project memories scoped per-project** (`processes.projectId` already exists, extend memory scope similarly). **Re-runnable:** retrofit machinery re-runs on schedule or on-demand to update substrate as project evolves — harness is maintained, not installed-once-forgotten. **Primary acquisition surface:** the in-depth analysis IS the user's first signal of value at project-connection time — turns a dead form-submission moment into "this is what Ditto sees about my work." **Where it lands:** medium-term parent brief "Project Onboarding & Battle-Readiness" with 4 sub-briefs (projects-schema + connection-as-process plumbing; analyser; retrofitter; project memory scope + cross-project promotion UX). **Dependencies:** Brief 212 (Workspace Local Bridge — needed for local-mac-mini retrofit execution), user's broader pipeline-spec `projects` table (`.context/attachments/pasted_text_2026-04-25_20-19-53.txt:3-19`). Brief 200 (workspace git server) is adjacent — Ditto can dogfood the retrofitter on its own workspace clone. **Reference docs touched:** `docs/insights/205-battle-ready-project-onboarding.md` (new), `docs/state.md` (this block). **Direct trigger:** user steer mid-conversation 2026-04-25. **Next step:** insight stays `active` until parent brief is written and approved. PM should sequence: (1) `projects` table brief first — substrate for everything, (2) onboarding parent brief depending on Brief 212 + the projects-table brief, (3) sub-brief decomposition. **Recommendation to user:** write the projects-table brief before the onboarding brief — onboarding has nowhere to land without the projects schema.

**Architect — Brief 212 design-decision resolution pass (2026-04-25, architect checkpoint #2):** User feedback "keep working the brief and resolve the design decisions — I am not best placed to resolve these" prompted a second pass resolving 14 architectural decisions inline + a delta reviewer round. **Decisions resolved:** (1) trust-tier semantics use REAL `TrustAction` enum values from `packages/core/src/db/schema.ts:110-116` (`pause | advance | sample_pause | sample_advance`) — supervised→pause, spot_checked-sampled-in→sample_pause, spot_checked-sampled-out→sample_advance, autonomous→advance, critical→tool-resolver-rejected-pre-DB-write, orphan→pause+`reviewDetails.bridge.orphaned=true` (no enum invention); (2) daemon process model: foreground first via `npx ditto-bridge start`, README ships launchd plist + systemd user-service templates, no menu-bar app at MVP; (3) tmux session lifecycle: daemon does NOT auto-create, `has-session` pre-flight, missing-tmux warning at startup, **`tmux send-keys -- <keys> Enter`** appends Enter automatically (user passes literal keys, no trailing newline); (4) subprocess defaults: `cwd=~`, env merged additively, SIGTERM-then-SIGKILL-after-5s, stdin=`/dev/null`, 4MB output cap with truncation marker; (5) one concurrent `running` job per device at MVP; (6) discriminated-union JSON Schema for `bridge.dispatch` written literally in AC #4 (`oneOf` with const-discriminator on `kind`); (7) precise `reviewDetails.bridge` audit shape including `stdoutTail`/`stderrTail` (last ~4KB scrubbed) — closes the review-surface-opacity gap; (8) state-machine transition triggers documented for all 8 states (queued/dispatched/running/succeeded/failed/orphaned/cancelled/revoked); (9) protocol versioning: JWT carries `protocolVersion: "1.0.0"`, major-mismatch HTTP 426, mid-flight cloud upgrade emits WebSocket close code 4426 + reason `protocol_upgrade_required`; (10) deviceId omission rules: routes to only-active-device, errors if multiple active; (11) admin nav location: `/bridge/devices` linked from existing `/admin` page as "Local devices" card; (12) `.env.example` URL fixed to path-based topology matching Brief 200 (`https://ditto.you/<workspace-slug>/api/v1/bridge/_dial`); (13) AC consolidation: 25→18 ACs (was 17, restored mobile-UX as discrete AC #15 per Reviewer P1-8), Insight-004 spirit honoured — one integration seam per AC, two deliberate consolidations on shared test surfaces (AC #14 daemon-handlers, AC #11 credential-lifecycle); **PM — Brief 211 opened: Workspace ChatPanel message-stomp regression (2026-04-21, pm checkpoint, post-CI-fix):** During PR #36's CI debugging session, identified a real product regression in PR #35's new `ChatPanel` (workspace chat surface): user sends a message → response renders → flashes back to blank within ~1s. User confirmed the symptom manually. Server-side healthy (`[/api/chat] Stream finished. Messages: 1` per send; mock LLM working on `/chat` page). Failure surface: 10 e2e specs in `packages/web/e2e/{blocks,pipeline,planning}.spec.ts` time out at `ConversationPage.waitForResponse()` because `[data-testid="assistant-message"]` never settles in DOM. **Triage path applied:** (1) Added `chat-input` + `send-button` testids to ChatPanel's textarea + SendButton (commit `936fae7`); (2) Added `new-chat-button` testid to sidebar's New Chat CTA + updated `ConversationPage.goto()` and 3 workspace.spec.ts tests to click it (commit `c26829c`) — workspace.spec.ts visibility tests now pass; (3) Skipped 10 affected describe blocks with `test.describe.skip` + TODO comments pointing at this brief (commit `dd7bfde`) — CI green at `test pass 4m32s` on PR #36. **Brief 211 opened (`docs/briefs/211-workspace-chatpanel-message-stomp-fix.md`, Status: draft)** with leading hypothesis: `workspace.tsx` lines 159–166 — the `setMessages(initialMessages)` reset effect lists `loading` in its deps, so the effect re-fires when `loading` transitions true→false after stream completes, calling `setMessages(initialMessages = [])` (memoized when active was empty), wiping streamed user+assistant messages. Architect to confirm or refute. Brief includes 11 ACs (un-skip the 10 specs + persistence-still-works check + manual repro at AC1), full diff inputs (workspace.tsx line ranges, chat-panel, thread-store, ai-elements/message), constraints (don't revert to prompt-input.tsx; preserve testid contract; preserve persistence). Engine scope: product-only (`packages/web/`). **Direct trigger:** user steer "Let's open a brief to fix this — I noticed that in the workspace, when ever I started a chat, it would render and then flash back to blank state" 2026-04-21. **Next step:** `/dev-architect` to refine Brief 211 from draft → ready (validate root-cause hypothesis, finalize fix approach, set Smoke Test acceptance gate). Then `/dev-builder` to implement, or `/drain-queue` will autoclaim once `Status: ready`.

**Documenter — User-Facing Legibility phase design complete (2026-04-20, documenter checkpoint):** Session produced **Insight-201** (user-facing legibility principle, four-category frame), **Insight-202** (Ditto-as-X before external-X), two research reports (`docs/research/user-facing-legibility-patterns.md`, `docs/research/memories-legibility-ux.md`), and **four briefs at Status: ready** (Brief 197 phase-level parent; Brief 198 memory write chokepoint refactor; Brief 199 memories projection + 2-stage safety filter + 54-entry regression corpus; Brief 200 workspace git-over-HTTPS server). Two Reviewer passes (pre-split pair, then post-split quad); first round found 3 CRITICAL (scattered memory write path; Railway deployment broke "files on laptop" premise; classifier mechanism unspecified); second round found 1 CRITICAL (ContentBlock reuse path) + 8 IMPORTANT + 4 MINOR. All CRITICAL + IMPORTANT fixes applied in-session; MINOR items folded into brief text. Session arc: started as 3-repo triage (browser-harness/autoreason/cabinet — all passed per `feedback_trend_triage.md`), pivoted when user flagged cabinet's filesystem-like UX property as architecturally significant. Scope expanded mid-session when user asked *"what about artefacts/emails/messages Ditto produces/receives?"* — reshaped Insight-201 to name four categories (outbound/inbound/generated/internal) and flagged artefact canonicalisation as prerequisite for Categories 1-3. User then asked *"why not just render from SQLite?"* — prompted honest reframe that I'd optimised for cabinet's surface feature (files on disk) rather than the underlying property (transparency/ownership); user affirmed continuous-projection model (Option C) but rejected GitHub dependency; Reviewer's "Railway container" catch forced Ditto-as-git-server architecture (Brief 200), which in turn generated Insight-202. Architect acted as Designer in-session (subagent Write permission denied twice — Researcher content reconstructed from subagent final-message summary; Designer killed before file-write, role-merged); Brief 199 AC #18 Designer re-review **waived by user authorization** on promotion to `ready` (documented in brief header; principle preserved). **Files written this session:** `docs/insights/201-user-facing-legibility.md`, `docs/insights/202-ditto-as-X-before-external-X.md`, `docs/research/user-facing-legibility-patterns.md`, `docs/research/memories-legibility-ux.md`, `docs/briefs/197-user-facing-legibility-phase.md`, `docs/briefs/198-memory-write-chokepoint-refactor.md`, `docs/briefs/199-memories-projection-and-safety-filter.md`, `docs/briefs/200-workspace-git-server.md`. **Files modified this session:** `docs/roadmap.md` (new "User-Facing Legibility" section between Phase 9 and Phase 10 with the four briefs + Category 1-3 blockers + Category 4 follow-on seams), `docs/landscape.md` (new "User-Facing Legibility & File-Backed Storage" section with 10 PKM/contrast entries + "Git Infrastructure" section with `isomorphic-git` + `@isomorphic-git/http-node` as `depend`), `docs/state.md` (this block). User-memory updates: `feedback_user_facing_legibility.md` (new), `feedback_grep_deployment_reality.md` (new), `MEMORY.md` index (both added). **Reference-doc audit:** `docs/landscape.md` updated; `docs/roadmap.md` updated; `docs/architecture.md` **deliberately NOT updated** — Insight-201 absorption criterion requires 2+ sub-briefs shipped (Brief 200 would be application #1 of Insight-202 once built; Brief 199 would be application #1 of Insight-201 once built; absorption premature until builders ship). `docs/dictionary.md` NOT updated — the new terms ("Memory Legibility File", "Sealed Memory", "Clone Credential", "Workspace Clone URL") are specified as Work Products IN Briefs 199/200; the Builder adds dictionary entries at build-time, not design-time. `docs/personas.md` / `docs/human-layer.md` / `docs/dev-process.md` / `docs/changelog.md` — no updates (no persona changes; Curate-as-seventh-job deferred until 2 sub-briefs apply the pattern; no phase closed). **Insight audit:** Insight-201 (new, active); Insight-202 (new, active). None absorbed; none archived. Insights cited in briefs (004, 050, 068, 111, 127, 180, 190, 196, 200) all remain active with no newly-triggered absorptions. **Open-question surfaced for PM:** Curate-as-seventh-human-job (proposed in Insight-201 + `memories-legibility-ux.md`) stays deferred until two sub-briefs apply the legibility pattern end-to-end. Future Category 1-3 sub-briefs are **blocked on artefact canonicalisation research** — that research pass is the next architectural unlock for outbound/inbound/generated comms legibility. **Compensating-control reminder:** Brief 199's waived Designer re-review should still happen before Build (treat the `memories-legibility-ux.md` UX as binding; deviations surface as architect callouts). **Retrospective (session-level):**

*What worked:*
1. **Trend-triage default held.** Original task was 3-repo triage — all three correctly flagged pass; user's genuine interest in cabinet's UX property drove the deeper work authentically rather than from over-scouting. `feedback_trend_triage.md` + Insight-196 doing the job they were saved for.
2. **User's "SQLite rendering?" push-back was the right forcing function.** Mid-session question surfaced that I'd optimised for cabinet's surface feature (files on disk) rather than the underlying property (transparent, divable, user-owned). Generalisation captured as session lesson even though the user ultimately authorised continuous projection — the question itself was the gift.
3. **Reviewer quad-pass caught real defects.** First round (pre-split pair): 3 CRITICAL — memory write path scattered across 16 files (not 1); Railway deployment broke "files on laptop" assumption; classifier mechanism unspecified. Second round (post-split quad): 1 CRITICAL (ContentBlock reuse path) + 8 IMPORTANT. Maker-checker separation earning its cost twice in one session. Pattern: Reviewer most reliably catches Architect hand-waves ("verify the env var / existing helper / framework before build") — those are the highest-yield grep-targets.
4. **Insight-004 split discipline applied organically.** When Reviewer-1 flagged the 17-AC memories brief was really a 16-callsite refactor + projection + classifier + server, splitting into 198/199/200 was natural. Each sub-brief independently testable with 12/18/16 ACs respectively; total cost 4-5 focused sessions, honestly flagged.
5. **Four-category frame emerged from user question, not pre-planned.** User's *"what about artefacts/emails/messages"* question reshaped Insight-201 correctly. The insight would have been narrow-and-wrong without it — it would have framed the whole legibility demand as an internal-state question when the persona-pain is actually highest on "what Ditto did on my behalf."
6. **Ditto-as-git-server (Insight-202) is a better answer than GitHub-push.** User's "don't want dependency on GitHub???" question directly generated the reframe. Insight-202 captures the generalisation: Ditto should self-provide user-facing capabilities before reaching for external providers. Brief 200 is application #1; a second application at a different user-facing seam unlocks absorption.

*What surprised:*
1. **Subagent Write permission denials, twice.** Researcher agent had Write denied (content reconstructed from the final-message summary); Designer agent killed before writing anything. The permission model for subagents is a genuine friction point in this harness configuration. Not fixed this session; flagged for a future `/update-config` pass if subagent delegation is part of the durable workflow. Workaround: Architect reconstructing research content from subagent summary; Architect acting as Designer in-session with documented compensating-control owed.
2. **"Files on your laptop" was a silent deployment assumption.** I wrote the initial brief pair assuming local-first deployment without checking `fly.toml`, Brief 100's completed Railway migration, or current container shape. Reviewer caught this as CRITICAL #2. The lesson became `feedback_grep_deployment_reality.md` — pre-publish grep of deployment reality joins the existing `feedback_grep_before_claiming_shared_namespace.md` discipline.
3. **"Lazy GitHub framing" was a real architectural blind spot.** When the local-files assumption broke, my default fix was "push to user's GitHub." User pushed back immediately — that was the right instinct. Ditto-as-git-server is more architecturally coherent AND matches the "no hard external-service dependency" principle Ditto already holds elsewhere (e.g., per-workspace provisioner, Network Service deployment). Insight-202 generalises this to *every* user-facing transport/storage surface.
4. **The "highest-value target for memories" claim in Insight-201's first draft was wrong.** Memories is the *cheapest* pilot seam (no canonicalisation prerequisite), not the highest-value. The high-persona-pain seams (Category 1 outbound comms — Rob's *"did you actually send that?"* anxiety) carry a bigger prerequisite. Claim softened on revision. Future insights that include "highest-value" claims deserve Architect interrogation before landing.

*What to change:*
1. **Before writing filesystem-touching briefs, grep the deployment config first.** Captured in `feedback_grep_deployment_reality.md`. Candidate for folding into `docs/dev-process.md` Architect contract next time that doc is touched — the discipline shares shape with Insight-200's observability-signal grep.
2. **"Highest-value" claims in insights/briefs need evidence gates.** When the first draft of Insight-201 said "memories is highest-value," there was no persona-pain evidence — just Architect convenience. User's artefacts question exposed it. Future insights that rank seams should either cite persona-pain evidence or not rank at all.
3. **Subagent permission config deserves attention before the next role-delegation-heavy session.** Two Write denials in one session cost real productive time (Designer killed mid-task; Architect had to role-merge + flag a compensating control). Flag for a dedicated `/update-config` audit pass.
4. **Architect-as-Designer role-merge discipline.** When subagent failure forces an in-session role merge, the compensating control (fresh-context re-review) should be named up-front in any artefact the merged role produces. Brief 199 AC #18 modelled this well; future role-merges should preserve the same clarity.

**Session did not change code or architecture.** Deliverables are design artefacts (4 briefs ready, 2 insights, 2 research reports). Next step: `/dev-pm` when ready to pick up the pilot build; **recommend 198 (chokepoint refactor) first** — small, mechanical, no dependencies, and unblocks 199. Brief 200 can build in parallel with 198 (no dependency). Brief 199 waits for 198. Pilot end-to-end user-facing legibility demonstrable once all three ship.

**Documenter — Browserbase research + Insight-200 parking mechanism close-out (2026-04-19, documenter checkpoint):** Session produced one research report, one insight, two brief updates, and one landscape refresh — all in service of a single decision: **don't adopt Browserbase now; park the decision behind named triggers; formalise the parking pattern as a reusable Architect technique.** **State-checkpoint verification:** Architect + Researcher checkpoints below are factually accurate. All four cited files exist (`docs/insights/200-interface-seam-plus-named-trigger.md`, `docs/research/browserbase-product-family.md`, `docs/briefs/182-browser-write-capability.md` updated §Open Questions §1, `docs/briefs/186-stagehand-agent-authoring.md` §Inputs item 11). Insight-200 is cross-referenced from state.md, the insight itself, Brief 182 OQ1 ("applies Insight-200"), and the research file's Flagged-for-Architect block — the cross-links are load-bearing, not decorative. **Reference-doc audit:** `docs/landscape.md` — updated in Researcher checkpoint (split bundled Stagehand/Browserbase entry into four; "Best fit" neutrality fix; pricing dated inline); no further drift. `docs/dictionary.md` — no updates: the new terms ("named-trigger parking", "interface seam") are Architect-role meta-process vocabulary, not cross-cutting Ditto domain terms; absorption into `docs/dev-process.md` (per Insight-200's own absorption criterion) is when dictionary entry becomes warranted. `docs/architecture.md` — no structural change; Brief 183's `BrowserRuntime` interface commitment stands. `docs/roadmap.md` — no phase boundary moved; Brief 182 remains Phase 9 adjacent. `docs/personas.md` / `docs/human-layer.md` / `docs/changelog.md` — no updates. `docs/dev-process.md` — explicitly NOT updated; Insight-200 sets its own two-count absorption gate. **Insight audit:** Insight-200 is the only new insight; stays `active`. None absorbed, none superseded. Reviewer verified novelty against 004, 023, 050, 051, 064, 068, 096, 163 — closest neighbour (Insight-051, agent-pluggability-must-be-proven) addresses a different moment (prove-the-abstraction-now vs park-the-implementation-selection). **Memory audit:** existing memory `project_reserved_adr_numbers_proposed.md` is adjacent to Insight-200 but addresses a different scope (ADR-number collisions across parallel in-progress sessions, not speculative future briefs). No memory update needed; the two mechanisms complement each other. **Roadmap:** no milestone reached, no phase closed. **Retrospective:**

*What worked:*
1. **The instinct-check became the durable artefact.** The Architect's first impulse was to pre-write a skeleton "Brief 197 — Hosted browser runtime" under Brief 182's family. Catching that impulse (and reflecting on *why* it was wrong rather than just suppressing it) produced Insight-200. The meta-pattern is: when the next instinct is to pre-commit, ask whether the architectural commitment is the interface or the implementation — if the interface is already committed, the rest is parking-with-triggers, not scheduling.
2. **Fresh-context reviews caught two self-contradictions in one pass.** Researcher review caught a "worth studying" neutrality slip and stale pre-existing "Best fit" landscape language. Architect review caught Trigger-D violating the insight's own applicability test — the insight's first application failed its own rule. Both were single-round catches; the maker-checker separation is earning its cost.
3. **Pricing date-pinning (2026-04-19) survived the review pass intact.** Reviewer flagged inconsistent date anchoring in landscape.md; the fix ("Pricing as checked 2026-04-19 — verify at the pricing page before any adoption decision") is now the standard phrasing for any decay-prone external dependency fact.

*What surprised:*
1. **The Researcher's initial landscape entry bundled Stagehand SDK with Browserbase Cloud** into a single line with "$99/mo" bolted on. Only when the human pointed at three specific product pages did the distinction become visible — Stagehand is OSS and Ditto already adopted it; Browserbase Cloud is a runtime transport; Browse CLI is a separate OSS package; Director is a hosted UI. Four distinct adoption decisions, not one. **Lesson:** when a vendor sells multiple named products, default to splitting the landscape entry on first mention; bundling hides decisions.
2. **Trigger-D's first draft felt concrete but wasn't.** "Heartbeat-lag or OOM attributable to browser runs" *reads* as observable; the reviewer's grep for `heartbeatLag` in the codebase exposed that no such field exists. The phrase "measurable" is not the same as "measured." **Lesson:** when Architect writes triggers for deferred decisions, run a grep pass for each trigger's signal mechanism BEFORE publishing — don't burn a P1 review slot on a self-contradiction the maker could have caught with one `Grep` call.
3. **Brief 182 Open Questions was unexpectedly thin.** The parent brief is otherwise detailed (282 lines, 14 inputs, 20 ACs across the family, full provenance table). Its Open Questions section was 3-line placeholder prose for each of 6 questions. The expansion of OQ1 alone added ~30 lines of concrete signal mechanisms — suggesting that Open-Question blocks in future parent briefs deserve the same treatment from the start, not just when a decision becomes load-bearing later.

*What to change:*
1. **Researcher default:** on first mention of a vendor in landscape.md, enumerate the vendor's discrete products as separate entries. Bundling is a smell, not a default.
2. **Architect discipline:** before publishing a brief update with observability-dependent claims (triggers, thresholds, metrics), grep the codebase for each cited signal — put pre-publish self-review ahead of the formal Reviewer pass. Insight-200 implies this; worth codifying in the Architect role contract at next dev-process.md touch.
3. **Parent-brief Open Questions hygiene:** when a parent brief opens an Open Questions section, default to the Insight-200 block template (named triggers + decision owner + artefact shape + research input) even for questions that don't *feel* load-bearing yet. Thin placeholders age poorly.

**Files written this session:** `docs/research/browserbase-product-family.md`, `docs/insights/200-interface-seam-plus-named-trigger.md`. **Files modified:** `docs/landscape.md` (Browser Automation section split + pricing dated + "Best fit" neutralised), `docs/briefs/182-browser-write-capability.md` (§Open Questions §1), `docs/briefs/186-stagehand-agent-authoring.md` (§Inputs item 11), `docs/state.md` (this block + Architect + Researcher checkpoints). **Not modified:** `docs/dev-process.md` (Insight-200 explicitly gates absorption), `docs/adrs/` (no ADR decisions taken), `docs/roadmap.md` (no phase movement), `docs/architecture.md` (no structural change). **Next step:** the session's deliverables are design artefacts, not code; no builder needed. `/dev-pm` for next work when you're ready to pick up the Phase 9 queue.

`docs/insights/198-narrow-regex-over-freeform-prose-deps.md` (when parsing freeform prose for machine-actionable signals, default to narrow extraction + human gate over generous parsing — generalizes ADR-035 doctrine 3); none absorbed by ADR-035 since the ADR is application-specific and the insights are broader principles. **Reference-doc gap audit:** `docs/dictionary.md` updated with three new entries (Autopilot (Dev Process), Brief State Mutex, Dispatch-Authorization Trust Boundary) at the alphabetical insertion point after "Autonomous"; no roadmap.md update needed. **Retrospective:** *What worked:* the four-round review process (architect rounds 1+2 → dev-review round 3 → builder round 4) caught successively deeper defects — round-3's 5-pass exhaustive audit found the squash-merge CRITICAL that two architect rounds missed, validating Brief 188's own "run BOTH /dev-reviewer AND /dev-review" maker-checker design. Adopting from Catalyst (vs reinventing) accelerated substantially. *What surprised:* the bootstrap paradox (brief 188 cannot be built by /drain-queue because /drain-queue is what it installs) is a unique meta-tooling characteristic worth flagging in any future "build the autopilot" brief; Catalyst's `pnpm typecheck` (no hyphen) vs Ditto's `pnpm run type-check` was a silent footgun that took multiple rounds to fully patch; the freeform `**Depends on:**` field in Ditto briefs was genuinely incompatible with Catalyst's structured `blocked_by` YAML, forcing the narrow-regex invention captured as Insight-198. *What to change:* the 5-pass dev-review skill is highly effective even on markdown design docs (not just code); worth invoking earlier in the design process for high-stakes briefs, not only at builder time. **Brief 188 NOT moved to complete/** — Status is `ready`, implementation is in working tree but PR has not yet been opened/merged. New `src/engine/self-tools/yaml-round-trip.ts` exposes pure `roundTripValidate(def)` that: (1) walks the definition tree to reject NUL bytes up-front with a dot-path to the offender, (2) `YAML.stringify`s, (3) `YAML.parse`s back, (4) canonical-JSON deep-equal against the original, (5) re-runs all four loader validators (dependencies, integration steps, step tools, model hints) on the reparsed value. Returns `{ ok: true, yaml }` or `{ ok: false, reason, path? }`. Wired into `generate-process.ts` after structural validation and before DB write; wired into `edit-process.ts` after structural validation and before version snapshot. 6 new tests cover happy path, NUL byte rejection with path, non-JSON-safe values (Function), dependency-cycle leak-through, YAML string output. 144/144 self-tools tests pass. **Files created:** `src/engine/self-tools/yaml-round-trip.ts`, `src/engine/self-tools/yaml-round-trip.test.ts`. **Files modified:** `src/engine/self-tools/generate-process.ts`, `src/engine/self-tools/edit-process.ts`. Brief: `docs/briefs/172-budget-spend-check-ordering.md`. **Brief 171 — Tool Output Credential Scrubbing (2026-04-16, complete):** P0 security fix closing credential-leak-via-tool-output. External APIs that echo auth tokens in error bodies (e.g. GitHub 401 with token prefix, Slack auth error with `xoxp-...`) previously flowed unredacted into `outputs.result` and then into LLM context, memories, SSE. New `src/engine/integration-handlers/scrub.ts` provides `scrubCredentialsFromValue()` — recursive walker over strings/arrays/plain objects, leaves Dates/Maps/Errors alone, redacts known secret values as `[REDACTED:{service}]`. Short secrets (≤4 chars) filtered out to avoid false positives. CLI handler now scrubs the PARSED result (not just log line) using `secretsFromAuthEnv(authEnv)` before building `outputs.result`. REST handler adds belt-and-braces scrub on the parsed response value (string-level scrub already existed on raw text). Tool-resolver dispatch boundary scrubs the final string returned to the LLM (defence in depth via `scrubToolOutput()` re-resolving auth) so a future handler variant that forgets to scrub cannot leak. Auth-resolution failure in the safety net is non-fatal — falls back to handler-scrubbed text. 13 new scrub tests + 2 CLI regression tests covering top-level strings, nested objects, arrays, Date preservation, multiple secrets, overlaps, >1MB strings. 96/96 integration tests pass. **Files created:** `src/engine/integration-handlers/scrub.ts`, `src/engine/integration-handlers/scrub.test.ts`. **Files modified:** `src/engine/integration-handlers/cli.ts`, `src/engine/integration-handlers/cli.test.ts`, `src/engine/integration-handlers/rest.ts`, `src/engine/tool-resolver.ts`. Switched `src/engine/integration-handlers/cli.ts` from `child_process.exec(commandString)` to `execFile(executable, args[])`. New `src/engine/integration-handlers/shell-tokenizer.ts` tokenises `command_template` into argv entries (whitespace splits outside quotes, single/double quotes group, `{placeholder}` always resolves to one argv entry regardless of value content). `buildCliCommand` in `src/engine/tool-resolver.ts` returns `{ executable, args }` instead of a shell string. `executeCli` accepts either `{ executable, args }` (LLM-invoked tools) or `{ command }` (YAML-authored integration steps; defensively tokenised). Credential scrub, timeout, buffer cap, retry semantics preserved. LLM-supplied argument values containing `;`, `&&`, `$(...)`, backticks, newlines, or unicode quotes now arrive at the target binary as a single verbatim argv entry — no shell interpretation possible. 23 new shell-tokenizer tests + updated cli tests; all 71 integration tests pass. **Files created:** `src/engine/integration-handlers/shell-tokenizer.ts`, `src/engine/integration-handlers/shell-tokenizer.test.ts`. **Files modified:** `src/engine/integration-handlers/cli.ts`, `src/engine/integration-handlers/cli.test.ts`, `src/engine/tool-resolver.ts`. New `DITTO_DEPLOYMENT` env var (`"public" | "workspace"`, defaults to `"workspace"` for safety) at `packages/web/lib/deployment.ts`. **Public mode**: `/` (root) bypasses auth so `<WelcomePage />` front door renders for unauth'd visitors; `/welcome` and `/admin` accessible. **Workspace mode**: `/welcome` and `/admin` hard-404'd at the edge by middleware (not just auth-gated — affirmatively not shipped on client installs); `/` falls through to the auth check and unauthenticated visitors land on `/login`. Two enforcement points: middleware (`packages/web/middleware.ts` — `BASE_PUBLIC_PREFIXES` + `PUBLIC_MODE_PREFIXES` + `WORKSPACE_MODE_BLOCKED_PREFIXES`) and server-component layout guards (`app/welcome/layout.tsx`, `app/admin/layout.tsx` call `notFound()` in workspace mode as belt-and-braces, also covers local-dev case where `WORKSPACE_OWNER_EMAIL` is unset and middleware bypasses auth). `app/page.tsx` branches on `isPublicDeployment()` so the WelcomePage fallback only appears in public mode. 6 new tests in `packages/web/lib/deployment.test.ts` (default, explicit values, case-insensitivity, unknown values, empty string). ADR-030 documents the decision (one flag rejected per-surface flags as too combinatoric). Type-check passes. **Files created:** `packages/web/lib/deployment.ts`, `packages/web/lib/deployment.test.ts`, `packages/web/app/welcome/layout.tsx`, `packages/web/app/admin/layout.tsx`, `docs/adrs/030-deployment-mode-flag.md`. **Files modified:** `packages/web/middleware.ts`, `packages/web/app/page.tsx`. **Branch:** `claude/fix-root-redirect-issue-CcukB`.

## What's Working

- **Web app (Briefs 039-042, 045-046)** — Next.js 15 App Router in `packages/web/`. Monorepo via `pnpm-workspace.yaml`. `pnpm dev` from root starts the web app. **Setup system:** first-run setup page at `/setup` with 5 connection methods. **Self streaming:** `selfConverseStream()` async generator, 5 LLM providers. Route Handler at `/api/chat` (AI SDK v6 `createUIMessageStream`) + SSE at `/api/events`. **Component Protocol (Briefs 045+050):** 22 typed ContentBlock types in `src/engine/content-blocks.ts` (16 original + 3 visual + 2 record/table + 1 ArtifactBlock — ADR-023 accepted). Unified block registry at `packages/web/components/blocks/` (22 components, exhaustive switch). **TextBlock renders markdown** via `react-markdown` + `remark-gfm` (headings, tables, code blocks, GFM). **ArtifactBlock** renders compact reference card in conversation with "Open" button → artifact mode. **Engine-connected artifact mode (Brief 050):** artifact host fetches `ContentBlock[]` from `/api/processes?action=getRunOutput&runId=` → renders through `BlockList` (no bespoke viewers, 720px max-width). `start_dev_role` outputs >500 chars auto-promote to artifact mode via `DelegationResult.metadata` (structured runId/processSlug). `transition-map.ts` extended. Parts-based message rendering via AI SDK v6 `UIMessage.parts`. Tool invocations show 7-state lifecycle. Custom data parts for content blocks, credentials, status. Session-scoped action validation via `handleSurfaceAction()`. Feed assembler enriches ReviewItems and ExceptionItems with ContentBlocks. Process outputs render via block registry. **Pipeline progress (Brief 053):** `ProgressBlock` populated from `activeRuns` in CompositionContext. `/api/processes?action=activeRuns` endpoint. `useHarnessEvents` invalidates `activeRuns` query key on pipeline SSE events (step-complete, gate-pause, gate-advance, run-complete, run-failed). Today + Work compositions prepend ProgressBlock for running pipelines. `use-pipeline-review.ts` hook: listens for `gate-pause`, fetches step output, exposes `pendingReview` state for inline review prompts. Transition map: `start_pipeline` → process_run panel context. **Conversation UI (Brief 058 — AI Elements adoption):** 8 adopted AI Elements components in `packages/web/components/ai-elements/` (Conversation with use-stick-to-bottom auto-scroll, Message with vivid dot + streamdown markdown, PromptInput with abort, Reasoning with collapsible shimmer, Tool with 7-state lifecycle, Confirmation for tool approval, Suggestion chips, Shimmer). Full useChat API surface: `dataPartSchemas` (4 Zod schemas, zero `as never` casts), `experimental_throttle` (100ms), `stop()`, `regenerate()` (hover retry on last message), `addToolApprovalResponse()`, `onData` (transient status), `onFinish`. Streaming markdown via `streamdown` (replaces manual rendering). Server: `consumeStream()` via tee for disconnect resilience, `transient: true` on status data parts. 6 shadcn/ui primitives. Design tokens from visual identity spec. **Workspace layout (Briefs 042+046):** Three-panel layout: sidebar (w-64, icon rail on medium screens) + center (feed + conversation + input) + right panel (w-72 collapsible, adaptive). **Workspace transitions (Brief 046):** Conversation messages from `useChat` render in centre column between feed and input. Right panel adapts to Self tool results via `TRANSITION_TOOL_MAP` (`transition-map.ts`): `generate_process(save=false)` → Process Builder panel (YAML structure, Drafting badge), `generate_process(save=true)` → process detail navigation, `get_briefing` → Briefing panel, `get_process_detail` → process trust context. Artifact Viewer panel for output review with lifecycle badge + Approve/Edit/Reject actions. Panel override clears on sidebar/Home navigation. Mobile (<1024px): artifact-review transitions show bottom sheet with swipe-to-dismiss. Auto-switch from conversation-only to workspace when first process created via Self (`workspace-events.ts` custom event bus). Progressive reveal: conversation-only for new users, workspace when processes exist. Sidebar: "My Work" (active work items with status dots), "Recurring" (domain processes with health indicators), "How It Works" (placeholder). Empty categories hidden. Process detail: 3 variants — living-roadmap (step timeline), domain-process (how it works + metrics + sparkline + trust control + activity log), process-runner (stepped wizard for multi-step human processes). Activity log: unified human+system timeline, filterable. Trust control: natural language slider ("Check everything" ↔ "Let it run") with evidence narrative. Engine View: developer-only toggle (Ctrl+Shift+E). Responsive breakpoints: ≥1280px full, 1024-1279px collapsed sidebar, <1024px hamburger+overlay. Process data API at `/api/processes`. All engine calls server-side. **Observability layer (Brief 056):** 6 semantic interaction event types (`artifact_viewed`, `composition_navigated`, `brief_selected`, `block_action_taken`, `review_prompt_seen`, `pipeline_progress_viewed`) recorded to `interaction_events` table via fire-and-forget `POST /api/events/interaction`. `useInteractionEvent()` hook with `navigator.sendBeacon()` + `fetch()` fallback + properties-aware debounce. Artifact mode tracks view duration. Workspace tracks navigation transitions. Pipeline review tracks response time. `briefs` table synced from markdown files via `syncBriefs()` (lazy from `/api/roadmap`). Self context enriched with `buildInteractionSummary()` in `loadWorkStateSummary()`. Implicit signals feed meta-processes only — NOT trust computation (trust.ts unchanged). `architecture.md` Layer 5 updated. **Real-time streaming (Brief 064):** Claude CLI `--include-partial-messages` enables `stream_event` parsing — `text_delta` → character-level text streaming, `thinking_delta` → live reasoning content. Deduplication guard (`receivedStreamDeltas`) prevents `assistant` complete message from doubling text. CLI internal tool calls (`content_block_start` tool_use → `tool-use-start`, `content_block_stop` → `tool-use-end`) surfaced through `self-stream.ts` → `route.ts` → browser. `extractToolSummary()` + `stripProjectRoot()` provide human-readable context (file paths, search patterns). 10 CLI tool display names in `tool-display-names.ts`. Activity grouping in `message.tsx`: consecutive CLI internal tools (Read, Edit, Grep, etc.) + reasoning grouped into collapsible ChainOfThought cards. Active: auto-open with contextual header ("Reading file..."). Complete: auto-collapse with summary ("8 steps — read file (5x), searched code (2x)"). Ditto's own tools render standalone. User toggle autonomy: `defaultOpen` (not controlled `open`), `userClosedRef` in Reasoning prevents forced reopening. Insights 124 + 125.
- **Storage** — SQLite + Drizzle ORM + better-sqlite3. WAL mode. Auto-created at `data/ditto.db`. Path resolved via `src/paths.ts` (`PROJECT_ROOT` anchored to monorepo root, not `process.cwd()`). (ADR-001). **Schema split by ADR-025 deployment topology:** `src/db/schema/engine.ts` (18 tables, re-exports from `@ditto/core`), `network.ts` (12 tables — people, fleet, docs), `frontdoor.ts` (7 tables — chat, verification, funnel), `product.ts` (9 tables — sessions, budgets, SLM, assets). Barrel re-export at `src/db/schema.ts` preserves all existing import paths. **Drizzle Kit migrations** replace hand-written SQL: `ensureSchema()` now runs `drizzle-orm/better-sqlite3/migrator`, baseline migration at `drizzle/0000_solid_blockbuster.sql` (45 tables). Pre-migration databases auto-detected and baseline stamped. `createTables()` in test-utils replaced with `migrate()`. `packages/core/src/db/schema.ts` is canonical source for engine tables — `delayedRuns` added, `processModels` moved to product schema, `decomposition` type fixed, `chainsProcessed`/`trustTierOverride` added to processRuns.
- **Process definitions** — 18 YAML processes in `processes/` (7 domain + 4 system + 7 standalone delegation roles). 22 template processes in `processes/templates/` (5 shared/cross-cutting + 4 Alex/Mira + 5 User Agent Gear 2 + 3 User Agent Gear 1 + 3 original non-coding templates). Parallel groups, depends_on, human steps, conditional routing (route_to/default_next). System processes have `system: true`. Standalone role processes (Brief 029, migrated Brief 031) are single-step `ai-agent` delegations with `config.role_contract` and `config.tools` (read-only, read-write, or read-write-exec — Brief 051).
- **LLM provider abstraction (Briefs 029+032+033)** — `src/engine/llm.ts`. Multi-provider registry: Anthropic, OpenAI, Ollama (via OpenAI-compatible API). Ditto-native types (`LlmToolDefinition`, `LlmContentBlock`, `LlmMessage` etc.) — no SDK types leak beyond `llm.ts`. `createCompletion()`, `extractText()`, `extractToolUse()`, `getConfiguredModel()`, `getProviderName()`. Tool format translation (Anthropic ↔ OpenAI) internal. `initLlm()` startup validation — fails clearly if `LLM_PROVIDER` or `LLM_MODEL` not set. Per-provider cost tracking ($0 for Ollama), cost calculated on actual model from API response. `LlmCompletionResponse` includes actual `model` from API. No hardcoded default model or provider. Provenance: Vercel AI SDK pattern, 12-factor app, Insight-060, Insight-062.
- **Model routing intelligence (Brief 033 + Brief 136)** — `src/engine/model-routing.ts`. Step-level model hints (`fast`/`capable`/`default`) in process YAML `config.model_hint`. `resolveModel(hint)` maps to provider-specific models (Anthropic: Haiku/Opus, OpenAI: gpt-4o-mini/gpt-4o; Ollama falls back to default). Model recorded on every `stepRun` (both advance and pause paths). `generateModelRecommendations(db)` analyzes 20+ completed runs per (process, step, model): recommends cheaper model when quality comparable (within 5%), recommends upgrade when quality low (<80%), and now detects SLM fine-tuning candidates (`type: "fine_tune_candidate"`) via readiness scoring. Current model determined from most recent 5 runs. Advisory only — no auto-switching. Process loader validates `model_hint` values. Provenance: Vercel AI SDK alias pattern, RouteLLM economics, Insight-175 (trust system as training data flywheel).
- **Claude adapter (Briefs 031+025)** — Role contract loading from `.claude/commands/dev-*.md` via `step.config.role_contract` (fallback to hardcoded prompts). Two tool categories merged at execution: codebase tools (`step.config.tools` → `readOnlyTools` or `readWriteTools`) + integration tools (resolved by harness from `step.tools`). Dispatches codebase calls to `executeTool()`, integration calls to `executeIntegrationTool()`. Confidence parsing from response text (`CONFIDENCE: high|medium|low`). Tool use loop (max 25 calls). Uses `createCompletion()` from `llm.ts`.
- **CLI adapter (Brief 016a)** — `src/adapters/cli.ts`. Spawns `claude -p` as subprocess. Loads role contracts from `.claude/commands/dev-*.md`. Parses CONFIDENCE from output. costCents: 0 (subscription-based). Provenance: ralph (subprocess), Paperclip (adapter pattern).
- **Script adapter** — Deterministic steps with on_failure
- **Integration infrastructure (Briefs 024+025+035+036)** — `integrations/` directory with YAML registry files (Insight-007). Registry loader (`src/engine/integration-registry.ts`) parses, validates, caches by service name. Supports tool definitions in YAML: `IntegrationTool` type with name, description, parameters, execute config (CLI command template or REST endpoint). `getIntegrationTools(service)` export. CLI protocol handler (`src/engine/integration-handlers/cli.ts`) executes via child_process.exec with retry (3 attempts, 1s/2s/4s backoff), JSON parsing, credential scrubbing. REST protocol handler (`src/engine/integration-handlers/rest.ts`) — native `fetch`, GET/POST/PUT/DELETE, auth header injection, credential scrubbing on all paths. `integration` executor type in step-executor switch. **Credential vault (Brief 035):** `src/engine/credential-vault.ts` — AES-256-GCM encrypted at rest, HKDF key derivation, per-(processId, service) scoping with UNIQUE constraint. Unified `resolveServiceAuth()`: vault-first, env-var fallback with deprecation warning. `processId` threaded through both execution paths (integration steps + tool use). CLI: `ditto credential add/list/remove`. `credentials` table in schema. Harness logs `integration.call` activities. Schema: `integrationService`/`integrationProtocol`/`toolCalls` on stepRuns. **Process I/O (Brief 036):** `src/engine/process-io.ts` — polling-based triggers (`startPolling`/`stopPolling`/`getPollingStatus`) and output delivery (`deliverOutput`). `source` and `outputDelivery` fields on `processes` table + `ProcessSourceConfig`/`ProcessOutputDeliveryConfig` types. Process loader validates service refs via `validateProcessIo()`. Heartbeat calls `deliverOutput()` after run completes (trust gate passed). Delivery payload includes collected approved step outputs + params. CLI: `ditto trigger start/stop/status`. Polling creates work items with `triggeredBy: "trigger"`. (ADR-005, Insight-065)
- **Agent tool use (Brief 025)** — Step-level `tools: [service.tool_name]` in process YAML. Tool resolver (`src/engine/tool-resolver.ts`) maps qualified names to `LlmToolDefinition[]` + execution dispatch function. Memory-assembly handler resolves tools → `HarnessContext.resolvedTools`. Claude adapter merges integration tools with codebase tools; dispatches integration calls via `executeIntegrationTool()`, codebase calls via existing `executeTool()`. Tool calls logged on `stepRuns.toolCalls` (name, args, resultSummary, timestamp). Process loader validates `service.tool_name` format against registry at sync time. Tools are Ditto-native (`LlmToolDefinition`), works with any LLM provider — MCP deferred (Insight-065). 2 integrations with tools: GitHub (4 CLI tools), Slack (2 REST tools). Provenance: ADR-005, Insight-065, Nango git-tracked approach.
- **Process loader** — YAML parsing, parallel_group containers, dependency validation, cycle detection, integration step validation (config.service required). Supports route_to, default_next, retry_on_failure fields (Brief 016b). Source/output_delivery validation against integration registry (Brief 036).
- **Integration generation (Brief 037)** — `ditto generate-integration --spec <file|url> --service <name>`. Parses OpenAPI 3.x spec (via `@apidevtools/swagger-parser`), emits valid Ditto integration YAML. Generate-then-curate pattern (Neon/Taskade). REST protocol only. Maps: operationId→snake_case name, summary→description, params→flat parameters, method→execute config. Classifies tools as read-only (GET) or write (POST/PUT/DELETE). PATCH skipped with warning. Handles: $ref resolution, nested object flattening (warns >1 level), missing operationId (skip+warn), deprecated ops (skip+warn), file upload (skip+warn), duplicate names (method prefix), enum values (in description), empty parameters (`{}`). Auth as placeholder only. Header comments with source, date, tool count, curation reminder. Provenance: Composio/Taskade/FastMCP/Neon patterns, Insight-071, Insight-072.
- **CLI** — citty + @clack/prompts. 15 commands: sync, start, heartbeat, status, review, approve, edit, reject, trust, capture, complete, debt, credential (add/list/remove), trigger (start/stop/status), generate-integration. TTY-aware, --json on listings. Unified task surface.
- **Work items** — workItems table (type, status, goalAncestry, assignedProcess, spawnedFrom). Conditional flow (Insight-039).
- **Harness pipeline** — 11 handlers: memory-assembly → identity-router → voice-calibration → step-execution → metacognitive-check → broadcast-direct-classifier → outbound-quality-gate → review-pattern → routing → trust-gate → feedback-recorder. **Brief 116 additions:** identity-router (pre-execution, resolves sending identity from step/process definition), voice-calibration (pre-execution, loads voice model for ghost mode), broadcast-direct-classifier (post-execution, deterministic audience-size lookup), outbound-quality-gate (post-execution, configurable house value checks, `alwaysRun: true`, non-bypassable). Metacognitive check (Brief 034b): post-execution self-review via LLM (maxTokens: 512). Auto-enabled for supervised+critical tiers, opt-in for others via `harness.metacognitive: true`. Flags issues for human review; does not re-execute. Shared `parseHarnessConfig()` in `harness-config.ts`. Review-pattern handler guards prior flags and merges reviewDetails. Routing handler (Brief 016b) evaluates route_to conditions via substring matching (Mode 1).
- **Trust gate** — 4 tiers: supervised, spot-checked (~20%), autonomous, critical. Deterministic SHA-256 sampling. Confidence override: `low` always pauses regardless of tier (ADR-011, Brief 016d). **Session trust overrides (Brief 053):** `session-trust.ts` — in-memory store keyed by runId. Overrides can only relax (supervised → spot_checked), never tighten. Builder/reviewer roles and critical-tier steps cannot be relaxed. Auto-cleared on run-complete/run-failed. **Broadcast forcing (Brief 116):** `audienceClassification === 'broadcast'` forces critical tier — absolute precedence, cannot be overridden. **Step-category trust overrides (Brief 116):** `stepDefinition.trustOverride` relaxes within process tier bounds (relaxation-only guard enforced).
- **Trust earning** — Sliding window (20 runs), conjunctive upgrades, disjunctive downgrades, grace period, simulation, override. (ADR-007)
- **Review patterns** — Maker-checker, adversarial, spec-testing. Retry with feedback injection.
- **Memory** — Three durable scopes: agent-scoped + process-scoped + self-scoped (ADR-003, ADR-016, Brief 029) + person-scoped (Brief 148, frontdoor-to-workspace bridge) + intra-run context (ephemeral, Brief 027). Salience sorting, token-budgeted assembly (2000 tokens durable, 1500 tokens run context), feedback-to-memory bridge. Self context loads person-scoped memories via email match for contextual workspace greetings.
- **Sessions (Briefs 029+030+099a)** — `sessions` table with full lifecycle: create, append turns, resume within timeout, suspend after idle (summary generated). Cross-surface resumption for workspace surfaces (ADR-016). Inbound sessions scoped separately — never cross-contaminate workspace sessions. 30min timeout for workspace surfaces, 24h timeout for inbound (async email thread continuity). DB-backed, not in-memory.
- **Cognitive framework (Brief 029, extended 034a+099a)** — `cognitive/core.md` (universal judgment layer) + `cognitive/self.md` (workspace extensions). `assembleSelfContext()` loads both for all surfaces. Consultative framing protocol, communication principles (competent/direct/warm/purposeful), trade-off heuristics, metacognitive checks (5 pre-action checks + teammate consultation guidance), escalation sensitivity, dev pipeline domain context. Identity substrate for the Conversational Self.
- **Conversational Self (Briefs 030+034a+040+043+044+053)** — `src/engine/self.ts` + `self-context.ts` + `self-delegation.ts` + `self-tools/`. The outermost harness ring: persistent identity, tiered context assembly (~6K token budget), `selfConverse()` conversation loop with tool_use delegation, session lifecycle. **26 tools total (19 original + 5 Brief 118 cycle tools + 1 Brief 079 search + 1 Brief 074 pause_goal):** Original 5 (`start_dev_role`, `consult_role`, `approve_review`, `edit_review`, `reject_review`) + 1 Brief 052 (`plan_with_role` — collaborative planning with read-only codebase tools, Architect gets `docs/`-restricted write) + 1 Brief 053 (`start_pipeline` — full pipeline trigger, async via `setImmediate`, returns runId immediately, optional `sessionTrust` overrides) + 7 Brief 040 (`create_work_item`, `generate_process`, `quick_capture`, `adjust_trust`, `get_process_detail`, `connect_service`, `update_user_model`) + 3 Brief 043 proactive (`get_briefing`, `detect_risks`, `suggest_next`) + 1 Brief 044 (`adapt_process`) + 1 Brief 068 (`assess_confidence` — structured confidence assessment, heuristic floor, conservative bias). **Confirmation model:** irreversible actions require explicit user confirmation. **Proactive engine (Brief 043):** `briefing-assembler.ts` queries 5 dimensions (focus, attention, upcoming, risk, suggestions). `risk-detector.ts` detects temporal, data staleness, and correction-pattern risks. `industry-patterns.ts` stores APQC-level business process patterns for 5 industries. `suggest-next` draws from all 9 user model dimensions + industry patterns + process maturity. Self proactively delivers briefings on user return (session gap detection). Risk signals woven into narrative — never says "risk" (Insight-073). Suggestions capped at 1-2, zero during exceptions. **User model:** 9 dimensions with behaviour tracking (`updateWorkingPatterns()` tracks login times, check frequency, preferred surface). **Onboarding (Brief 044):** `processes/onboarding.yaml` — system process with 5 steps (gather-basics, identify-first-pain, reflect-understanding, propose-first-process, first-real-work). `adapt_process` tool writes run-scoped definition override on `processRuns.definitionOverride` — template stays durable. Guards: validates against process-loader schema, cannot remove/reorder protected steps (running/waiting_review/approved), system processes only, optimistic locking. Heartbeat re-reads override at each step boundary. 3 new ContentBlock types: `knowledge_synthesis`, `process_proposal`, `gathering_indicator`. Knowledge synthesis card (editable, corrections feed back to Self). Process proposal card (plain language steps, approve/adjust). Self speaks first for new users. `cognitive/self.md` extended with onboarding conversation guidelines + AI coaching principles. **Masked credential input:** secure field at `/api/credential`. **Integration registry:** `ConnectionMetadata` type on IntegrationDefinition. Self-stream extended with `structured-data`, `credential-request`, and onboarding content block event types. Self decision tracking, self-correction memories, cross-turn redirect detection unchanged. Telegram bot routes free-text through the Self.
- **Human steps** — `executor: human` suspends execution, creates action work item with input_fields, `aos complete` resumes with human input.
- **Pattern notification** — After 3+ corrections of same pattern, read-only notification surfaced. Precursor to Phase 8 "Teach this".
- **Parallel execution** — Promise.all for parallel groups, depends_on resolution
- **Heartbeat** — Routes through harness. Sequential + parallel. Human step suspend/resume. Conditional routing (route_to/default_next). Retry with feedback injection (retry_on_failure). Routing skips mark non-target siblings as "skipped". Output delivery hook after run completion (Brief 036).
- **Harness events** — `src/engine/events.ts`. Typed event emitter: step-start, step-complete, gate-pause, gate-advance, routing-decision, retry, step-skipped, run-complete, run-failed. Provenance: Trigger.dev event pattern.
- **Agent tools (Briefs 031+051)** — 5 tools: read_file, search_files, list_files (read-only), write_file (read-write), run_command (read-write-exec). Path traversal prevention, secret deny-list, symlink protection. `run_command` executes allowlisted shell commands via `execFile` (no shell interpretation): pnpm (run/test/exec/install --frozen-lockfile), npm (run/test), node (file paths only), git (read-only ops). npx entirely blocked. Executable+subcommand allowlist enforced. Output scrubbed for secret file references. 120s timeout, 10MB buffer cap. Builder and Reviewer use `read-write-exec` for verification evidence. Exported as `readOnlyTools` (3), `readWriteTools` (4), and `execTools` (5). Command output parsed into ContentBlocks (ChecklistBlock for test results, AlertBlock for type-check/timeout, CodeBlock for generic output) via `parseCommandOutputBlocks()` in self-stream.ts.
- **DB schema enforcement** — `ensureSchema()` runs Drizzle Kit migrations at startup (web instrumentation, CLI sync). Schema changes: edit Drizzle schema → `pnpm db:generate` → commit migration file. Single source of truth — no hand-written SQL to maintain.
- **Debt tracking** — `docs/debts/` markdown files. `pnpm cli debt` to list.
- **Dev process** — 7 roles as skills. Brief template (with composition Level column, Insight-068). 68 active insight files (156 compiled knowledge layer — new this session). **Known issue:** 2 pre-existing number collisions at 071/072 and 164 (from separate sessions). Needs renumbering cleanup. 165 collision resolved (token efficiency → Insight-170). Brief 115 collision resolved (pricing strategy → Brief 119). 31 archived. 42 research reports. 12-point review checklist. Distributed knowledge maintenance (Insight-043): each role maintains docs it reads, Documenter does cross-cutting audit.
- **Dev pipeline** — `claude -p` orchestrator + Telegram bot. Full Claude workspace on mobile. (Brief 015). Engine-integrated: `processes/dev-pipeline.yaml` runs 7 roles through the real harness with conditional routing (Brief 016c). Telegram bot routes free-text through the Conversational Self (Brief 030): `selfConverse()` assembles context, converses via LLM, delegates to dev roles via tool_use. Engine bridge (Brief 027) for explicit `/start` commands: `startProcessRun()` + `fullHeartbeat()` loop, review actions. Memory, trust, feedback all active.
- **Review actions (Brief 027)** — `src/engine/review-actions.ts`. Shared approve/edit/reject logic extracted from CLI commands. Pure engine functions (no TTY, no process.exit). Step-level granularity via `findWaitingStepRun()`. Used by both CLI commands and Telegram bot.
- **System agents (Brief 014a+014b+021+104)** — 5 system agents running through the harness pipeline: trust-evaluator (wraps Phase 3 code, spot-checked), intake-classifier (keyword matching, supervised), router (LLM-based via `llm.ts`, supervised), orchestrator (goal-directed — decomposes goals into tasks, routes around paused items, confidence-based stopping; supervised), process-validator (4-check quality gate for library curation, supervised — Brief 104). `category: system` + `systemRole` on agents table. System agent registry dispatches via `script` executor + `systemAgent` config (Insight-044). `startSystemAgentRun()` for programmatic triggering.
- **Goal-directed orchestrator (Brief 021+022)** — Decomposes goals into child work items using process step list as blueprint. `orchestratorHeartbeat()` iterates spawned tasks, routes around trust gate pauses to independent work. Confidence-based stopping: low confidence triggers escalation (Types 1/3/4). CLI: scope negotiation in `capture`, goal tree in `status`, escalation display. Schema: `decomposition` on workItems, `orchestratorConfidence` on processRuns.
- **Process templates (Brief 020)** — 3 non-coding templates in `templates/`: invoice-follow-up (4 steps, 1 human), content-review (3 steps, all AI), incident-response (4 steps, 2 human). All include governance declarations (trust, quality_criteria, feedback). Loaded as `status: draft` via `aos sync`. Process loader reads from both `processes/` and `templates/`.
- **Auto-classification capture (Brief 014b)** — `aos capture` auto-classifies work item type (keyword patterns) and auto-routes to best matching process (LLM). Falls back to interactive @clack/prompts on low confidence. System processes filtered from routing targets.
- **Test infrastructure (Briefs 017+054)** — vitest + 400 unit tests across 24 test files + Playwright e2e (14 tests, 4 spec files). Mock LLM layer (`MOCK_LLM=true`) with regex-keyed canned responses for deterministic e2e testing. DB reset endpoint, page objects, CI workflow. vitest covers process-loader, trust-diff, heartbeat (including orchestratorHeartbeat), feedback-recorder, trust computation, system agents (registry, classifier, orchestrator decomposition + scheduling + escalation, step dispatch), integration registry (8 tests), CLI protocol handler (6 tests), memory-assembly intra-run context (6 tests, Brief 027), agent tools (9 tests + 47 run_command tests, Briefs 031+051), standalone YAML structure (13 tests incl. read-write-exec, Briefs 031+051), LLM provider abstraction (31 tests, Brief 032), metacognitive check + harness config + flag survival (21 tests, Brief 034b), model routing + hint resolution + recommendations (20 tests, Brief 033), tool resolver + tool name validation + authorisation (8 tests, Brief 025), REST handler + auth injection + credential scrubbing (10 tests, Brief 025), credential vault + scoping + auth resolution (11 tests, Brief 035), process I/O + polling + delivery + validation (10 tests, Brief 036). Real SQLite per test via Drizzle migrations (no mocks, no hand-written SQL). Anthropic + OpenAI SDKs mocked at module level. `pnpm test` runs in ~3.8s.
- **E2E verification (Brief 020)** — Full work evolution cycle verified: capture → classify → route → orchestrate → execute → human step → resume → review → trust update. All 6 architecture layers proven working. Report at `docs/verification/phase-5-e2e.md`.

- **Brief 215 — Projects + Runner Registry substrate (2026-04-26, complete + reviewed + post-review fixes shipped):** First seam of Brief 214 cloud-runners phase. Engine-core: `packages/core/src/runner/{kinds,state-machine,interface,resolution,webhook-schema,index}.ts` — pure resolver, 9-state dispatch SM (queued→dispatched→running→{succeeded|failed|timed_out|rate_limited|cancelled|revoked}), Zod webhook discriminated-union, RunnerAdapter contract. `packages/core/src/projects/invariants.ts` — pure status-transition invariants (analysing→active requires defaultRunnerKind + enabled runner row). Ditto product layer: `src/engine/runner-registry.ts` (in-process Map), `src/engine/runner-dispatcher.ts` (chain walk + per-attempt audit + harness_decisions row per Insight-180), `src/adapters/local-mac-mini.ts` (RunnerAdapter shim over Brief 212's `LocalBridge`), `src/engine/projects/seed-{data,on-boot}.ts` (idempotent agent-crm + ditto seeds). Web: `/api/v1/projects` CRUD scaffold; `/api/v1/projects/[id]/runners` POST returns 501 for cloud kinds (sub-briefs 216-218); `/projects` index, `/projects/new`, `/projects/[slug]`, `/projects/[slug]/runners` mobile-first admin pages. /admin gets a "Projects" card. Migration `0012_projects_runners.sql` (idx=11, journal entry tag `0012_projects_runners`; Brief 212 sits at idx=10 tag `0011_local_bridge`). 48 new tests (35 core + 13 integration), all pass. Root type-check clean. Pre-existing core type-check failures in `outbound-quality-gate.test.ts` (last touched commit 0e04886, unrelated to this brief). 1942 root tests pass — no regressions. **Review outcome:** APPROVE WITH FIXES — reviewer flagged 1 H + 2 M + 3 L + 3 N. **Post-review fixes (2026-04-26, shipped):** **H1** runners route precheck used undefined `r.kind` → fixed to `WHERE projectId AND kind`; **M1** dispatcher writes were ad-hoc → every status write now flows through `transitionDispatch` (queued→dispatched→running→terminal); added `queued + fail → failed` SM event for adapter-throw cases; **M2** `harness_decisions.reviewPattern = ["runner-dispatch"]` discriminates dispatcher rows from review-gate rows; **L1** engine-boot wiring (`packages/web/instrumentation.ts`) registers the local-mac-mini adapter into the registry + runs `seedProjectsOnBoot()`; Brief 212 §"After Completion" gained a wiring obligation note; **L3** `seedProjectsOnBoot()` wraps check+insert in `db.transaction(...)`; **N1** advisory orphan-`processes.projectId` count + warn at engine boot; **N2** `/projects/new` form default for `harnessType` aligned to schema default `'none'`; **N3** `briefSourceValues` normalised to underscore-form (`ditto_native`, `github_issues`); **AC #12** e2e Playwright spec at `packages/web/e2e/projects.spec.ts` (mobile-first 375×667, kind-selector enabled/disabled assertions, no-horizontal-scroll check). **AC #11** local-mac-mini adapter is the documented placeholder shim (bridge: null) — wiring obligation captured in Brief 212's §"After Completion" item 0. Final verification: root `pnpm run type-check` clean; `pnpm test` 1967 passed (was 1957) + 9 skipped, no regressions. **Files:** see brief §"What Changes" + the post-review fixes summary. **Next:** `/dev-pm` for next work.

- **Paperclip Evaluation + Hire-a-Specialist Architecture Stack (2026-04-20, design complete, awaiting build):** Major architectural session. Produced the design substrate for activating the L2 Agent primitive as a user-facing hirable specialist, grounded in a deep re-evaluation of Paperclip (paperclipai/paperclip — 56.4k stars, 6-week stale landscape entry refreshed). **Artifacts produced:** `docs/landscape.md` Paperclip entry refreshed (schema + primitive catalog + adapter contract evolution + UX surface inventory + layered relevance + explicit anti-patterns); **ADR-036** Database Tier Strategy (SQLite-per-workspace permanent; Network tier → Postgres at named triggers ≥50 active users / ADR-033 RSI in prod / p95 >50ms sustained 24h; file-level tier split folded into Brief 202; extends ADR-001); **ADR-037** Hired Agents Primitive (activates L2 Agent as user-facing specialist; YAML-primary storage per Insight-201; conversational hire as default; core/product-shaped field boundary; no `reports_to`, no `company_id`; uses ADR-007 four-tier trust vocabulary); **ADR-038** Self-Supervised Agent Dialogue (Self manages agents; direct user↔agent dialogue with always-watching Self; five interjection verbs Ask/Flag/Pause/Escalate/Propose — closed enumeration; observation-rate bands keyed on ADR-007 tiers; three-voice conversation UX; extends ADR-016); **ADR-039** Hired-Agent Memory Scope (new `hired-agent` scope_type; Self reads all, owning agent reads own, no default cross-agent reads; - **Brief 098a — Pulse Engine + Chain Execution (2026-04-07, complete)** — Alex's continuous operation loop. Phase 12: Network Agent Execution. **`ChainDefinition` type** added to `packages/core/src/harness/harness.ts` — minimal engine primitive (trigger, process, inputs). Variable substitution in product layer. **`chain-executor.ts`** (new): reads chain definitions from completed process, creates delayed runs (delay triggers), schedule records (schedule triggers), logs event handlers as deferred (event triggers, 098b activates). Variable substitution (`{personId}` → actual value) with dotted path support. **`pulse.ts`** (new): continuous operation loop registered as cron job. On each tick: (1) scan due delayed runs → start them, (2) scan completed runs for unprocessed chains → execute. Configurable via `PULSE_INTERVAL_MS` env var (default 5 min). Idempotent — DB-backed state (`chainsProcessed` flag on processRuns, `status` on delayedRuns). Overlap guard (`pulseRunning` flag). **`delayed_runs` table** (id, processSlug, inputs, executeAt, status, createdByRunId, parentTrustTier). **Trust inheritance (AC9):** Chain-spawned runs inherit the more restrictive of parent and target trust tiers via `parentTrustTier` on delayed_runs → `trustTierOverride` on processRuns. `moreRestrictiveTrust()` helper. **Heartbeat wired:** `processChains()` called after output delivery on process completion. Errors logged, do not fail the run. **Layer classification:** chain definitions = L1 (Process), pulse = L2 (Agent/Heartbeat). **22 tests.** 868 total (48 files). Type-check clean. Reviewed: PASS. **Files created:** `src/engine/chain-executor.ts`, `src/engine/pulse.ts`, `src/engine/pulse.test.ts`. **Files modified:** `packages/core/src/harness/harness.ts`, `packages/core/src/harness/index.ts`, `packages/core/src/index.ts`, `src/engine/harness.ts`, `src/engine/heartbeat.ts`, `src/engine/process-loader.ts`, `src/db/schema.ts`, `src/db/index.ts`, `src/test-utils.ts`. **Next:** Brief 098b (inbound email + status composition + weekly briefing).

- **Insights 160-162 (2026-04-07/08, active)** — Three interrelated design insights captured during 098b/099 sessions. **Insight-160 (trust context):** Trust tiers determined by context, not uniformly supervised. Alex→User = autonomous. Alex as professional = autonomous (quality-gate safety net, Ditto admin reviews). User's business = supervised. System gates = critical. 14 process templates reclassified. **Insight-161 (email/workspace boundary):** Email is arms-length, workspace is embedded. Natural graduation when complexity exceeds email. Notification routing table by user deployment state. **Insight-162 (email relationship lifecycle):** User intent taxonomy (6 types), adaptive onboarding (reasoning, not schedule), Self IS the intent classifier (19 tools), proactive composition via `createCompletion()` (not `selfConverse()` — avoids session pollution).

- **Brief 102 — Goal-Level Reasoning & Action Boundaries (2026-04-08, complete)** — Orchestrator evolution: LLM-powered goal decomposition + dimension map clarity assessment + system-enforced action boundaries. Phase 11+: Orchestrator Evolution. **`GoalDecomposition` types** added to `packages/core/src/goal-decomposition.ts` — engine primitive (SubGoal, DimensionMap, GoalPhase, GoalDecompositionResult discriminated union). Exported from `@ditto/core`. **`dimension-map.ts`** (new): `assessClarity()` evaluates 6 dimensions (outcome, assets, constraints, context, infrastructure, risk_tolerance) via heuristic signal matching. `isDecompositionReady()` gates on outcome dimension (must be clear or partial). `getClarityQuestions()` returns questions for vague/unknown dimensions. **`goal-decomposition.ts`** (new): `decomposeGoalWithLLM()` — gathers process inventory, industry patterns, optional web search (capped at 2), builds structured prompt, calls LLM via `purpose: "analysis"`, parses structured JSON response, tags sub-goals as `find`/`build` based on process inventory keyword matching, groups into phases when >8 sub-goals. Graceful fallback on LLM parse failure. **`action-boundaries.ts`** (new): `getToolSetForContext()` returns system-enforced tool sets — `front_door` (research-only: search_knowledge, assess_confidence, web_search, person_research, draft_plan), `workspace` (full tools: 21 tools), `workspace_budgeted` (workspace + 3 budget tools). `determineActionContext()` derives context from workspace/session state, not prompts. `filterToolsForContext()` for tool filtering. **Orchestrator modified:** New LLM decomposition path when goal/outcome has no processSlug. Existing 1:1 fast path (goal + processSlug → step decomposition) unchanged. `OrchestrationResult` extended with `goalDecompositionResult`. **17 AC all pass.** 978 tests (55 files). Type-check clean. Reviewed: APPROVE with non-blocking flags (F1 front-door tools fixed, F3 direct db import acceptable in product layer, F4 purpose vs model_hint terminology noted). **Reference doc drift:** architecture.md orchestrator description should note LLM decomposition capability. **Files created:** `packages/core/src/goal-decomposition.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/dimension-map.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/goal-decomposition.ts`, `src/engine/action-boundaries.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/dimension-map.test.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/goal-decomposition.test.ts`, `src/engine/action-boundaries.test.ts`. **Files modified:** `packages/core/src/index.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/orchestrator.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/orchestrator.test.ts`. **Next:** Brief 103 (find-or-build routing) now buildable.

- **Brief 103 — Find-or-Build Routing & Goal-Level Trust (2026-04-08, complete)** — Find-or-build routing for orchestrator sub-goals. Phase 11+: Orchestrator Evolution. **Three-tier routing** in `routeSubGoal()`: (1) Process Model Library (`findProcessModel()` — keyword matching against `templates/`), (2) existing process match (`matchTaskToProcess()` — confidence ≥ 0.6), (3) Build meta-process (`triggerBuild()` — LLM research → generate process → save → first-run validate). **Build depth enforcement** via explicit `buildDepth` counter — harness rejects when ≥ 1. **First-run gate:** generated processes start as `draft`, promote to `active` on successful first run, archive on failure (max 1 retry, then escalate with evidence). **Goal-level trust** (`resolveSubGoalTrust()`): effective tier = more restrictive of goal and process tier. Critical tier and builder/reviewer roles cannot be relaxed. **Output threading** (`threadOutputs()`): LLM-based extraction/shaping between completed and dependent sub-goals. `reThreadOutputs()` for user correction (AC14). **Bundled reviews** (`collectForBundledReview()` + `isReviewBoundary()` + `presentBundledReview()`): reviews at phase boundaries (all find or all build sub-goals in dependency tier complete), not per-step. Individual feedback per sub-goal output (approve/edit/reject). **Concurrent build dedup:** keyword-based dedup key, in-flight builds tracked, duplicates wait. **Goal cancellation** (`cancelGoal()`): in-progress sub-goals paused, build-in-progress processes archived, completed outputs preserved. **Cost observability:** all routing decisions logged with path, confidence, reasoning, costCents, costCategory (free/cheap/expensive). **18 AC all pass.** 1015 tests (59 files). Type-check clean. Reviewed: PASS with 5 flags (1 medium fixed: archiveBuildInProgress goalId filter; 4 low fixed: comment cleanup, status mapping comment, dedup key noted). **Reference doc drift:** architecture.md orchestrator description should note find-or-build routing. dictionary.md needs terms: ProcessModelMatch, GoalTrust, BuildResult, BundledReview. ADR-015 should note Build meta-process reactive trigger from orchestrator. **Files created:** `src/engine/system-agents/process-model-lookup.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/build-on-gap.ts`, `src/engine/goal-trust.ts`, `src/engine/output-threading.ts`, `src/engine/bundled-review.ts`, `src/engine/goal-trust.test.ts`, `src/engine/output-threading.test.ts`, `src/engine/bundled-review.test.ts`, `src/engine/system-agents/find-or-build-routing.test.ts`. **Files modified:** `src/engine/system-agents/orchestrator.ts`. **Next:** Brief 104 (library curation pipeline) now buildable. Invoke `/dev-documenter` for retrospective, or `/dev-pm` for next work.

- **Brief 104 — Process Model Library Curation Pipeline (2026-04-08, complete)** — Quality pipeline for the Process Model Library. Phase 11: Process Model Foundation. **`processModels` table** added to `packages/core/src/db/schema.ts` (engine primitive) with: slug, name, description, industryTags, functionTags, complexity (simple/moderate/complex), version, status lifecycle (nominated/testing/standardised/review/published/archived), processDefinition (YAML as JSON), validationReport, source. Type unions: `ProcessModelStatus`, `ProcessModelComplexity`, `ProcessModelSource`. Synced across `src/db/schema.ts`, `src/db/index.ts` (ensureSchema), `src/test-utils.ts`. **`process-validator.ts`** (new): unified system agent performing 4 checks in one pass: (1) edge-case testing (name, steps, required fields, dependency refs, circular deps), (2) compliance scanning (3 secret patterns, 3 PII patterns, trust tier recommendation), (3) efficiency analysis (hardcoded URLs, consecutive same-executor consolidation, quality criteria, description length), (4) duplicate detection (Jaccard similarity >70% threshold, merge recommendation). Produces structured `ValidationReport` with per-check evidence. Registered as system agent via `ensureReferencedSystemAgent()` in process-loader (ADR-008 pattern). **`library-manager.ts`** (new): `nominateForLibrary()` creates entry + starts curation process run, `getLibraryModels()` filters by industry/function/complexity, `publishToLibrary()` requires admin approval (cannot be bypassed) + bumps version + archives old, `archiveModel()` soft delete. **`findProcessModel()` updated (AC9):** Now async, queries `processModels` DB table first (published models), falls back to filesystem `templates/` if DB empty. Orchestrator `await`s the call. **`library-curation.yaml`** (new): 5-step process (nomination → validate → standardise → admin-review → publish) running through the harness. **Reference docs updated:** ADR-008 (14th system agent: process-validator), ADR-015 Section 7 (process-validator added, "no new agents" policy replaced), architecture.md (14 system agents). **Validation types** (`ValidationCheckResult`, `ValidationReport`) defined in `packages/core/src/db/schema-process-models.ts`, re-exported via `@ditto/core`. **11 AC all pass.** 1049 tests (61 files). Type-check clean. Circuit breaker trips after N consecutive failures (default 2, configurable). Each failed workspace individually rolled back to its own pre-upgrade image before counter increments. DITTO_NETWORK_URL verified BEFORE machine update (no wasted restart). Concurrency guard (in-memory, single-process safe). Idempotent resume (skips workspaces already at target image). **Alerting:** `src/engine/workspace-alerts.ts` — webhook POST with 3-attempt exponential backoff retry, structured console.log fallback. **Schema:** `upgrade_history` + `upgrade_workspace_results` tables. **API:** `POST /api/v1/network/admin/upgrade` (202 Accepted, async), `POST /api/v1/network/admin/rollback`, `GET /api/v1/network/admin/upgrades`, `GET /api/v1/network/admin/upgrades/:id` (status polling). - **Brief 151 — Outreach Dedup, Context Injection, and Staged Dispatch Wiring (2026-04-14, complete)** — Fixes 261-duplicate "Reached out to Tim" production bug. Three mechanical fixes: (1) **Dedup safety net** — `sendAndRecord()` rejects duplicate outreach to same person within same process run + enforces per-person daily cap of 3 in 24h. Suppressed decisions logged to activities table (Insight-184 corollary 3). (2) **Context injection** — cycle auto-restart injects `recentOutreach` array into next run's inputs so LLM SENSE/ASSESS steps see what was done. (3) **Staged dispatch wiring** — `dispatchStagedAction` callback wired on harness context so `crm.send_email` (staged: true) actually dispatches after quality gate approval.
